<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uittreksel.html>uittreksel</a> (48257)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uittreksel.html>uittreksel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uittreksel.html>uittreksels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uittreksel.html>uittrekseltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitvechten.html>uitvechten</a> (12882)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">utevechten</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vechten.html>vechten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitvechten.html>uitvechten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reach a solution or an end through fighting; to fight it out
<ul><li><b>1799</b>, Samuel Richardson, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:geschiedenis.html>Geschiedenis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Karel Grandison</i> (= tr. of <i>The History of <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> Charles Grandison</i>), part 4, <a href = vnd.unilang:johannes.html>Johannes</a> Allart (publ.), pages 314 and 315.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>Wel</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meent.html>meent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:elkander.html>elkander</a> aankeeken, <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paar.html>paar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zotten.html>zotten</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alleen.html>alleen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zagen.html>zagen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:opdat.html>opdat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> zoo <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> ſpreken, den ſtrijd <a href = vnd.unilang:zouden.html>zouden</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uitvechten.html>uitvechten</a></b>?</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Well, and you don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> suppose that <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:looking.html>looking</a> at one another like a pair of fools, when <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> only watching, so that <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a>, so to speak, would <b>fight out</b> the battle?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1988</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:tijdschrift.html>Tijdschrift</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:theologie.html>theologie</a></i>, page 284.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>Onze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kennis.html>kennis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ervan.html>ervan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeer.html>zeer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beperkt.html>beperkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vervalst.html>vervalst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> propaganda-oorlogen <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koloniale.html>koloniale</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:machten.html>machten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:elkaar.html>elkaar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uitvechten.html>uitvochten</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Our knowledge about it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> seriously limited and also falsified by the propaganda wars that the colonial powers <b>fought out</b> with each other.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***uitverkoop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitverkoop.html>uitverkoop</a> (9539)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">uit-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verkoop.html>verkoop</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitverkoop.html>uitverkoop</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitverkopen.html>uitverkopen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitverkoop.html>uitverkoopje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sale (a period of reduced prices)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> avocado's <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <b>in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitverkoop.html>uitverkoop</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dus.html>dus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paar.html>paar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kilo.html>kilo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gekocht.html>gekocht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:guacamole.html>guacamole</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The avocados <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <b>on sale</b>, so I bought a few <a href = vnd.unilang:kilos.html>kilos</a> to make <a href = vnd.unilang:guacamole.html>guacamole</a> with.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">uit-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">out-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waaien.html>waaien</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to blow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, <span class="ann-pos">of wind</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitwaaien.html>uitwaaien</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go out in windy weather, particularly into nature or a park, as a means of refreshing oneself and clearing one's mind</li></ol>

***uitzending.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitzending.html>uitzending</a> (5247)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitzenden.html>uitzenden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to send out, broadcast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitzending.html>uitzending</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitzending.html>uitzendingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitzending.html>uitzendinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">broadcasting</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Broadcast, also programme or episode.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitzitten.html>uitzitten</a> (12881)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zitten.html>zitten</a></i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitzitten.html>uitzitten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remain for the duration of; to sit for the duration of, to remain seated for the duration of</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to serve time (of a prison sentence) until completion</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In the sense “to serve time until completion”, the term means that one <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> not received a <a href = vnd.unilang:pardon.html>pardon</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> escaped and <a href = vnd.unilang:remains.html>remains</a> at large.

***underdog.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:underdog.html>underdog</a> (17279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">under-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dog</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:underdog.html>underdog</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:underdogs.html>underdogs</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A competitor thought unlikely to win.
<ul><li><b>2004:</b> <i>The New Yorker,</i> 30 August 2004, p.40
<dl><dd>In Athens, the Americans are <b><a href = vnd.unilang:underdogs.html>underdogs</a></b> to the Chinese and the Canadians <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the Canadians!</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2014</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:jacob.html>Jacob</a> Steinberg, "<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.theguardian.com/football/2014/mar/09/manchester-city-wigan-athletic-fa-cup">Wigan shock Manchester City in FA Cup again to reach semi-finals</a>", <i>The Guardian</i>, 9 March 2014:
<dl><dd>The visit of a Championship side would not normally send a shiver down their spine but they <a href = vnd.unilang:knew.html>knew</a> that Wigan <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:underdogs.html>underdogs</a></b> who would <a href = vnd.unilang:snap.html>snap</a> at their <a href = vnd.unilang:heels.html>heels</a> and that they possessed a potent bite if they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> not kept on a firm leash.</dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">little guy</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>Somebody at a disadvantage.</li>
<li>A high swing wherein the person pushing the swing <a href = vnd.unilang:runs.html>runs</a> beneath the swing while the person being <a href = vnd.unilang:pushed.html>pushed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> at the forward limit of the arc.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:underdog.html>underdog</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>  <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>

***underlay.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a> (19514)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">underleyen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">underleċġan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a>, prop, support</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">under-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lay</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">onderleggen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lay or put under</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">unterlegen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">underlägga</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">simple past tense of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">underlie</i></span></span></li></ol>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">underlays</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">underlaying</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">underlaid</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To lay (something) underneath something else; to put under.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To provide a support for something; to raise or support by something laid under.
<dl><dd><i>to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a></b> a cut, plate, or the like, for printing</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To put a tap on (a shoe).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mining<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive, intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of a vein, fault, or lode</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To incline from the vertical.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">hade</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">underlei</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">under-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lay</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">underlays</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A layer (of earth, etc.) that lies under another; substratum.</li>
<li>A soft floor covering that lies under a carpet.</li>
<li>Anything that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> underlaid.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">printing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A piece of paper pasted under woodcuts, stereotype plates, etc. in a form, to bring them up to the necessary level for printing.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:lyrics.html>Lyrics</a>; or more specifically, the way in which <a href = vnd.unilang:lyrics.html>lyrics</a> are assigned to musical notes.
<dl><dd><i>The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a> 3 <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unclear in <a href = vnd.unilang:handel.html>Handel</a>'s manuscript.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

***universe.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> universe (2245)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b>universe</b>
</p>
